How to create a email system protocol by yourself?


1. You have a center server
2. http://mail.a_user.com wants to do a registration, you send a random string to that url, if that user send back the right random code, registrate successful. (We do this check every 1 hour, if the target server is not responsive, we save any email that going to send to there until it alive again. Or we could simply remind sender the receiver is not online 
3. When other people want to send a mail to mail.a_user.com, they send email to your center service first, then you send it directly to http://mail.a_user.com server.
4. If http://mail.a_user.com wants to send a email to others, they send request message to you, you send random message back, if they can provide right random message, you help to send that message out.



Or 



you simply define one single POST API, let anyone wants to send message to you, send post request to you.

Something like:

Request: {title, content, author_email_url}

Response: {success, error}


And another thing you have to do is make a 20MB size of spam,AD,normal text AI classifier


_____________________


How to create a email system protocol by yourself? 


You simply define one single POST API, let anyone wants to send message to you, send a post request to your subdomain, for example, email.your_domain.com:

Something like:

Request: {title, content, author_email_url}

Response: {success, error}


And another thing you have to do is make a 20MB size of "spam,AD,normal" text AI classifier


#idea #yingshaoxo

买个60L的预烧恒温电热水器，可以解决所有洗澡问题


_____________________


一种恒温热水器的实现：

1. 一个大浴缸，侧边新增一个向外突出的方槽用来放 热得快。
2. 准备一个温度传感器，一个水位传感器。温度传感器比水位传感器低3厘米，水位传感器放在理想水面高度。
3. 当水位条件满足，热得快开始通电加热，当温度条件满足，热得快断电。
4. 有条件的还可以做自动加水、放水。
5. 为安全考虑，供电 可用 有便捷开关的电排插。

> 额外零件：220v转为5v的降压板、5v可编程控制器、5v控制220v的继电器

#idea #yingshaoxo

总统选举 流程优化：


人口几乎恒定，

每人一个选举周期内只能投一票给一个人，

但这个票可以实时变化，上一秒可以投给A，下一秒又可以转给B，

在一个选举周期结束时，数据冻结，生成1个G的txt选举数据，供全国人民检验。

类似格式为：

People_ID    Target_Peopel_ID

另外可附带一个小txt：

Target_Peopel_ID    Policy_Or_Hope


#idea #president #selection #yingshaoxo

_____________________


Presidential election process optimization:


 The population is almost constant,

 Each person can only vote for one person in an election cycle.

 But this vote can change in real time. It can be voted for A one second and transferred to B the next second.

 At the end of an election cycle, the data is frozen and 1 G of txt election data is generated for inspection by the people across the country.

 A similar format is:

 People_ID Target_People_ID

 In addition, a small txt can be attached:

 Target_Peopel_ID Policy_Or_Hope


 #idea #president #selection #yingshaoxo

I looked stackoverflow help docs, it says if I have questions about stackoverflow, I could ask it here.

Because, as you know, a programming language is also a tool, a built-in library is also a tool.

For example, if someone ask you, "How can I write a socket client?"

There would have a lot of answers, 

someone would say "You could use Python to do that..."

Another would say "You could use rust to do that..."

And even more, some would even recommand a library "You could use flask to do that..."

There would always have people to recommend different tools or librarys.

Is the "How can I write a socket client?" question illegal according to stackoverflow guidline?

_____________________


We just have another Python Package Manager called YPPM:



YPPM is similar to javascript npm or yarn. 

It uses package.json to do the underlying work. 

And it has a friendly command line interface, which supports auto completion in real time.

And even more, it can compile a python program into a binary executable file by using pyinstaller or nuitka with one command.

Oh, you can even use 'yppm create_a_new_project' to select project templates, for example, a front-end and back-end seperate project. This is similar to vite in javascript.


_____________________


一个工具人，如果比你强，你将无法驾驭它，不一定为你工作

如果比你弱，你就不用期待它能做连你都做不到的事情了

#tool_people #rule



If a tool is better than you, you will not be able to control it and it may not necessarily work for you.

If it's weaker than you, you don't have to expect it to do things that even you can't do.

#tool_people #rule

选365个人，每个人成为一个行业的专家或者在那个行业工作

365个人，是有联系的，在一个远程匿名群，每人一年只能发一条请求信息，一天里只能有一个人发送请求信息

当群组其他人收到请求，花一天或多天帮忙实现该请求

365群组上还有一层匿名机构，每个群组一年只能向上级发送一次请求，上级一年也只能向所有群组发送一次请求

上级会根据下级的请求，综合判定应该提出什么样的请求给所有群组，这个请求为该年的总愿望

#超越小团体 #Super_Group

Auto_everything database daemon:

1. It loads txt data into memory.
2. It controls data read, edit, append, delete. Only one client doing operations at one time, it is a single process.
3. When it communicate with client, it mainly sends and receives text data by line. Then treat it like json and so on.
4. It will save memory data into disk for every 15 minutes.

#super_database

NFC tag has 3 parts: A chip, an antenna, and the inlay.

Which means NFC is a microcontroller.

RFID is the base of NFC.

RFID card size is 81x54x1 mm. Which less than 1 cm.

If you add sun power to it, when you add RFID to skin, it'll always have power and it will keep running to spy or even control you.

#NFC #RFID


___


NFC标签由3部分组成：芯片、天线和嵌体。

这意味着 NFC 是一个微控制器。

RFID是NFC的基础。

RFID 卡尺寸为 81x54x1 毫米。 不到1厘米。

如果你给它加上太阳能，当你给皮肤注射RFID后，它就会一直有电，并且会持续运行来监视甚至控制你。

#NFC #RFID

Auto_Everything 的用户协议：


第一次运行本library，会弹出一个用户协议命令行，需要输入 y 才能跳过。(该配置会存到~/.auto_everything/config.json里, key == user_agree)


用户协议大致是：

本library是由yingshaoxo无偿开发的。

做好事提升开发效率的同时，肯定会触犯到其他团队或者旧有势力，所以他们肯定会想方设法的404本libray。

举个例子，github就无缘无故地封了我的账号。

希望大家在使用时广为传播本library，这样敌对垄断势力就无法封禁本library了。

本library作为一个工具，不对任何用本工具产生的副作用负责任。

同时因为我们采取了MIT协议，所以使用本工具的人可以不受限制的拿本工具做任何事情。

你同意吗？(y/n)

真实世界的p2p钱包(类似区块链钱包)：


你花钱买 别人服务器上的数字，你期待 以后用那个数字 买到别人的产品

你也可以 租服务器 卖给别人服务器上的数字，以后别人 用服务器上的数字 买你的产品

当然你也可以 把程序数据、钱包数据放在你本地电脑，类似于账本，上面记录着 某某给了你多少钱，以后可以从你那儿取多少钱


#p2p #wallet

How to make a new browser?


1. vue style file for HTML. For example, main.vue, page1.vue, you can do relative import to call JavaScript(or mini_python, only handle Json and get post request) functions or HTML elements. And custom HTML elements looking by using css inside vue file.

2. In browser client, treat the whole vue project as an dict object, rendering it as a picture. Handle keyboard and touchscreen information, change graphics accordingly. Send get, post request according to its script.


#pure #python #broswer #yingshaoxo

IP v4 has limited address is a lie.

255×255×255×255=10 digitals number

But if you add one more 255 before old ipv4, you can get:

255×255×255×255×255=13 digitals number=one trillion level IP addresses

If you use 10 255 number as new IP standard, you get almost unlimited IP addresses 

#ipv4 #upgrade #yingshaoxo

Policies (一个良好平台的政策)

1. Compliance with Laws and Regulations (独裁政权的法律本身就是邪恶的，不用遵守)
2. User Safety (我们建议你用虚拟机运行软件，这样就算是病毒也不怕，所以我们不对网站的软件负责)
3. Intellectual Property, Authenticity, and Private Information (你视为珍宝的源码、知识财产为什么要泄漏到公共网络？如果是被间谍或者脑机接口所偷，对不起，我们无力对抗。)
4. Spam and Inauthentic Activity on GitHub (我们欢迎任何内容，包括垃圾内容，可能会置底，但如果你付费上架，我们更欢迎。)
5. Site Access and Safety (我们告诉我们的用户，正如你遇到的每个人都可能是坏人一样，你遇到的每个链接也可能是诈骗链接，谨慎点击。)
6. Services Usage Limits (我们不是万能的)
7. Information Usage Restrictions (我们一般不会用你的数据，除非匿名训练AI)
8. Privacy (我们不会主动泄漏用户数据，除非被黑客攻击。)
9. Excessive Bandwidth Use (我们推荐用户使用磁力、云盘等工具分享文件。)
10. Advertising on GitHub (我们很开放，我们不在意用户在我们平台发广告)
11. User Protection (我们建议用户拿出100%的谨慎对待平台的任何内容。同时对于自己的数据，要经常备份。)

By agreeing this policy, you agree to give up any rights to lawsuit our platform.

#business #policy #yingshaoxo

TTS hard coding method:


Word to Sound directly, but with software to control it's strongth, tune, pause length between words.

The strongth is actually the relative audio volume between a word, a sentence. (Or audio volume line)

And the tune will need you to change each word length.

Audio Line: 40 50 70 100 (volume %, from low to high)

Audio length: 1 1.8 1 (word relative length, "how are you?")

Audio pause length: 0.1 0.1 (word pause relative length for "how are you")


#tts #yingshaoxo

_____________________


TTS hard coding method 2:


1. Text map to 64k mp3 audio

2. Use ",." symbol to separate text, so you get less repeated text data

3. When you got 1GB of data, you get a well functioned TTS

> You could even use speech recognition to collect audio to text dict data.

> By using this method, you could get almost 100% accurate TTS for your voice 


#tts #yingshaoxo

They let you specify app permissions first, then cut permission one by one. I mean they will only allow you to use graphs in the end.

And in the end, they will even remove some functions from linux kernel level.

If you know google play app development, you would know what I am trying to say.

How to control a car with keyboard?

Direction keys "up, down, left, right" to control the car direction. 

One pressure(weight) sensor used to increase power, if you stop hitting it, it will stop power supply. (It could be the up key, or the down key in another direction)

Accelerate slowly by adding constant power.

Another stop key is used when you hit it, if you hit it, the car will slow down quickly by stop power and using hardware brake.

It is similar to QQspeedDrifters, but the drift key is used to cut off power and use hardware brake directly.

自行车没有电力系统，仍然轻松实现了刹车系统，好厉害

#car #control #keyboard #yingshaoxo

Local DNS for HTTP:


1. Set up a http service that have one API: "register_namespace(username, password, namespace, forward_http_service_url)". namespace can be any string.

2. Local DNS service parses header "namespace" for every request that sends to it, forward that request to registered namespace forward_http_service_url.

3. If you have http GET needs, you could pass "METHOD: GET" to header, so the end target will return you pure text as HTML code.


#idea #yingshaoxo

# Report System


We hope we can be a platform that do not censorship anything.
But if we have to compromise for living (last choice), then, we could do this:

1. If anyone's product get 'reported as harmful one', we hide that product for one month.

2. After one month, we'll recover that product automatically.

Why we do this?

If someone care, then there would always have people to do report (false or true).

If nobody care, there would have no report.

极限压缩版 自然语言 预测下一个词：

abcdef g
ace g
ad g

字符串中间省略相同长度字符，线性统计下一个大概率字符，硬编码记忆

#ai #ml #yingshaoxo

_____________________


升级版：

概括上一串字符为某个概念，下一串字符只能从另外几个可能的概念里获得

前一个抽象概念词或句子 -> 后一个抽象概念词或句子

概念从大到小，最终落到字单符级别

先写文章、再写段落、然后写句子、然后写单词、最后写字符

If you want to do it, you have to parse context text concepts tree first, who did what, who ask what

The answer is like: 是什么、为什么、怎么办？

#ai

_____________________


实际数据取得：

先有一大串连续自然语言文本，然后把它分为sub_sentence，给每个sub_sentence用一串更少字符代替，更少字符+标点的合集变成了新的txt文本

然后基于新的更小文本，你再压缩一次，每个句子对应一个更小文本，变成新txt

然后基于新文本，每个段落变成更小文本，变成新txt

然后每篇文章变成一个一段话，变成新txt

然后一个章节变成一句话，变成目录词

最后所有文本变成一句话，变成书名


接着你搜索时，先搜小文本，精准匹配，如果有，recursive 补全子文本。如果没有，继续在更大文本搜索。


_____________________

如果去掉它，用前一个字符或word仍能大概率预测出下一个词，那它就可以被去掉

You need a sentence transformer:

A sentence transformer is a loop function that sometimes add a word between words, sometimes remove a word between words

The final goal is to make that sentence looks good as an answer. (human understandable and related to context)


_____________________


It is pobabally equal to:

{"before_word*after_word": "center_word"}

This is used to correct sentence.


_____________________


Or it might be:

1. copy global_dict(memory) as a new one
2. update global_dict based on context information
3. predict

or 

1. use global_dict do the generation first
2. use context_dict do a word level grammer fix on the generated sentence
3. the final text would have right sentence that related to context

# Yingshaoxo machine learning ideas

## For natual language process
We treat every char as an id or tensor element

In GPU based machine learning algorithm, you will often do things with [23, 32, 34, 54]

But now, it becomes ['a', 'b', 'c', 'd']


### For text summary
For the self attention mechanism, it is using word apperance counting dict. You could think it as a dict, multiple key link to one same value, for all those multiple key string, if a word show up a lot of time, it is likely a important word.
(You can think this as a TV show, for the same envirnoment, if a person only show once, it is not the main character, it is not important. But if a character show a lot times, you can almost see it at any eposide, then it is a important character)

For one sequence or list, If its importance number less than average(half of 'its sequence importance sum'), you remove it

Or you could do this: if that word does not appear again in the following sentences of the input_text in your database, you treat it as not important text.


### For translation
long sequence (meaning group) -> long sequence (meaning group)

what you do -> 你干什么
It depends on -> 这取决于

(It depends on) (what you do) -> 这取决于 你干什么

meaning group can be get automatically, all you have to do is count continues_words appearance time. the more time a continuse_words appear, the more likely it is a meaning group

It all can be summaryed as "divide and conquer"


### For question and answer
For context information extraction, you have to use the question. If one sentence of the context should at the bottom of the question, you keep it, otherwise, you remove it

Then, for the other context, you do a simple sort

### For text generation
one char predict next char
two char predict next char
...
one word predict next word
two words predict next word
three words predict next word
...

when you use it, use it from bottom to top, use longest sequence to predict the next word first.

> the more level you make, the more accurate it would be.

> It is dict based next word generator, so the speed is super quick

> This method was created by yingshaoxo. it only need cpu than gpu. it can beat gpt4 with an old computer if you have big dataset (30GB) and big memory to hold the dict.

General Strong AI algorithm:

1. When it hear/see/feel anything, it converts it into bytes(or text)
2. Bytes can be audio/video and so on
3. Bytes will merge into one single hidden layer as context or memory dict
4. For each time step, the hidden layer or memory will mainly represent a video/image/text/audio and so on (that's why you could play audio in your mind, play video in your mind, see graphics in your mind, it is called imagination)
5. The text based representation is advanced thoughts, the lower level hidden states is under subconscious
6. Hidden states can be able to get used to generate actions for each time step
7. Action will cause new data generation in reality
8. New data may change hidden states in return
9. It is a loop

> All data here is a sequence data, or stream.

#ai #idea #yingshaoxo

自制火药枪：

1. 准备火药子弹。一个子弹样的容器，里面填充火药，屁股露一个火药点。(火药=6nitrate+4sugar)

2. 准备一个枪管，可以是大钢筋中间钻空，可以是小水管

3. 把子弹放进去，枪管背后加一个中间钻孔的小硬币焊死、点火器，密封枪管后座。点火器可以是打火机、电脉冲发生器。

4. 点火发射

> 如果想要连发，需要加弹夹、把手。用分贝检测芯片控制子弹的固定，一旦高音量点燃，松开子弹让它飞。

> 或者氢气推动的气枪

#DIY #gun #yingshaoxo

流浪人口救助系统：


1. 准备一个连接公交站的大厂房(政府福利项目，没有房租)

2. 厂区分为4部分。1为室内区，用于放置电冰箱和储物柜。2为公开帐篷区，可随意睡觉。3为农场，用于种植高产作物以及养蚯蚓。4为养殖区，用于养母鸡。全厂房顶有太阳能板，内设有厕所、洗衣房、洗澡房。

3. 冰箱储物柜+储物柜 是一套信用系统，分为公有库与私有库。如果你要拿公有库的东西，需要看提供方30秒的广告(提供者可以是其他流浪汉)。

4. 冰箱储物柜只用来储存食物。如果有流浪汉免费提供可食用垃圾给农场喂蚯蚓，那我们给他的积分系统加分，他们可凭积分多换取几个鸡蛋。

5. 公有库、私有库可以是知识库，比如数字内容，我们存到硬盘。


#idea #流浪汉救助系统 #yingshaoxo

5v自加压气枪原理：


1. 普通气枪一支
2. 5v可编程芯片、温度传感器、压力传感器、加热器
3. 蒸汽瓶预热，自动控温，压力达到目标值就降温，反之就升温
4. 气枪通过高压蒸汽发射出子弹


#自加压 #气枪 #idea #yingshaoxo

___

Theory of 5v self-pressurizing air gun:


1. An ordinary air gun
2. 5v programmable microcontroller, temperature sensor, pressure sensor, 5v heater
3. The steam bottle is preheated and the temperature is automatically controlled. When the pressure reaches the target value, it will cool down, otherwise it will heat up.
4. Air guns fire bullets through high-pressure steam


#self_pressurizing #air_gun #idea #yingshaoxo

人脸检测算法：

图片模糊缩小减少差异像素后，寻找两个对称，大框左右对称，小框基于中心垂线镜像左右对称，小框在大框里面。

为什么在 传统教育体系下 开小差、成绩最差、整天东想西想的 同学 最容易成功呢？

1. 学校教育是愚民教育的一环，知识导向和价值取向本身就是错的，学得越深入越容易变成庸民(俗称打工仔)

2. 统一的学校教育 和 社会舆论控制 会把所有人的目光 都集中在一件事情上，在同一个时间。所以越深信学校教育的人，越是会踏入一条竞争激烈的道路

_____________________


Google 的 ChatAI 有对 新词 做实时tokenizing

换句话讲，它把新词按照习惯相对位置，放在了回答中

它整个模型不是记忆的死词，而是上下文词的相对位置

举个例子，a b c a，这个规律

如果你把问题看作是 a b，答案是 c a

那么当问题变为 j b，答案顺应变为 c j

#google #ai

一个小问题，电机可以反向充电

类似手摇发电机

为什么市面上没有脚踩式发电自行车？

一种既能脚踩充电，又能靠储存的电力前行的自行车，为什么市面上没有？

#question #yingshaoxo

___

电机靠电力驱动旋转，

根据能量守恒转换定律，不应有大损耗

同理，你脚踩旋转电机，发电

根据能量守恒转化定律，也不应有大损耗

最终，市面上没有 脚踩发电自行车+正常电动车 的组合式产品，有可能就是坏人比较多，或者就是你们都不知道电机可以反向发电

#idea #yingshaoxo

How to use python to make a linux mobile system or phone?

How to make a mobile phone and mobile phone system based on MIT license projects?

1. Prepare micro_python project. It is MIT licensed.
2. Change pyboard CPU to PC CPU. Change pyboard memory to 32GB, change pyboard storage to 2TB.
3. Make a never stop python loop. And let it run when connect to power. 
4. Use python to send signal and drive LED screen.
5. Use python to read keyboard or touch screen signal.
6. Use python to send sound signal to speakers.
7. Upgrade that python loop into a bash shell.
8. Let python be able to handle hardware USB signals.
9. Create pure image based graphic library with python, so it can sent out graphic signal stream directly to LED screen.
10. Use python to make a desktop launcher, which has terminal, file explorer, browser, 3 tabs.

#mobile #os #MIT #python #yingshaoxo
